### Post by t0p on 2011-08-10
Trying to burn a folder full of stuff to back it all up.  I've tried both Brasero and K3b, and neither will do the trick, even though they both successfully simulating the burn.  Not getting much feedback on why the burn won't work - K3b says OPC failed, probably doesn't like the medium.  I've tried to do the job with plenty of CDs now, so I don't think it's down to dodgy disks.

I'm including the debug info files, so maybe someone more knowledgeable can tell me what's what.  Sorry I can't just stick 'em up there as attachments, but for some reason my computer or the website won't let me.  Cheers!

/usr/bin/genisoimage -gui -graft-points -volid Transmetropolitan -volset  -appid K3B THE CD KREATOR (C) 1998-2010 SEBASTIAN TRUEG AND MICHAL MALEK -publisher  -preparer  -sysid LINUX -volset-size 1 -volset-seqno 1 -sort /tmp/kde-t0p/k3bAR8566.tmp -rational-rock -hide-list /tmp/kde-t0p/k3brm8566.tmp -joliet -joliet-long -hide-joliet-list /tmp/kde-t0p/k3btK8566.tmp -no-cache-inodes -full-iso9660-filenames -iso-level 3 -path-list /tmp/kde-t0p/k3bIw8566.tmp

### Post by TeoBigusGeekus on 2011-08-10
Create an iso of the folder
```
mkisofs -o imagename.iso -J /path/foldername/
```
and then try to burn it to a cd with wodim
```
wodim -v dev=/dev/cdrw /path/imagename.iso
```
Replace cdrw with whatever applicable (dvd, cd, sr0, etc)

---

### Post by t0p on 2011-08-12
**TeoBigusGeekus:** Thanks so much for the advice!

I went to /dev to see what my system calls my CD drive, and there were 3 options: /dev/cdrom and /dev/cdrw.  The disks I've been trying to write to have all been CD-Rs, and there was no /dev/cdr.  So, I tried that wodim command, set to write to /dev/cdrw - no joy.  Then I did it again, set to write to /dev/cdrom... and it worked!!  So now I can back up stuff on CDs.

Thanks, TeoBigusGeekus!  You saved my life!  (Well, you didn't actually save my life - if my HDD went down and took all my precious data with it, I woulda been distraught, but I don't think I would've actually *died*... but you helped me out plenty.]  Cheers!!
